**Lessons learned** (→ `Playbook/lessons-learned.md`):
1. **Halt discipline saved capital** — 0 additional SL vs minimum 6-8 prevented over 6.5h. Rule preservation commitment inviolable.
2. **OBI spoof density** — 22+ spoofs in 6h = extreme distribution day marker. Use as regime classifier (>15 spoofs/6h = distribution dominant).
3. **CVD absorption patterns** — sustained +\$10M+ buy pressure absorbed by price = distribution confirmation. Price action ultimately overrides flow when sellers dominate book.
4. **Short-squeeze dynamics** — CVD negative with price rising = short-covering rally. Often reverses если CVD doesn't flip positive in 2-3 cycles.
5. **Sweep+reclaim failure rate** — 0/4 early reclaims, 1/5 late reclaim = 20% success rate in distribution regime (vs 60%+ in range/bull). Adjust expectations.
6. **1H Protocol zones matter** — early zones (75567, 75440) correctly priced as resistance/support на reversals = good validation of protocol methodology.
